    2.sh $jd npm_install
    3.sh $jd ＃查看网页IP和端口

commit fdb8e971138b09bcdf4eba98c4e16460ad5ae6bc
Author: Zhenjian Zhang <itdesk.zhang@gmail.com>
Date:   Sat Mar 27 13:42:08 2021 +0800

    解决backnas命名带：，导致windows底下乱码
    
    之前使用我的备份，导致乱码的，可以用底下命令修复
    
    1.cd 到你的备份目录
    2. for i in `ls ./ `;do a=$(echo $i | sed "s/:/_/g") && mv $i $a ;done
    
    这样就修复好了
    
    Signed-off-by: Zhenjian Zhang <itdesk.zhang@gmail.com>

commit ef7a6889c015b51837627c27648205bab3f2daff
Author: Zhenjian Zhang <itdesk.zhang@gmail.com>
Date:   Thu Mar 18 14:10:06 2021 +0800

    统一jdcookie文件和推送文件
    如果更新完成以后并发还是失败，请按底下办法修复，不再单独通知
    1.备份/usr/share/jd_openwrt_script/script_config/jdCookie.js
    2.备份/usr/share/jd_openwrt_script/script_config/sendNotify.js
    3.rm -rf /usr/share/jd_openwrt_script/script_config/jdCookie.js
    4.rm -rf /usr/share/jd_openwrt_script/script_config/sendNotify.js
    
    然后更新脚本sh $jd update_script && sh $jd update && sh $jd
    
    5.去这里把参数填好
    /usr/share/jd_openwrt_script/script_config/jdCookie.js
    /usr/share/jd_openwrt_script/script_config/sendNotify.js
    
    6.开始跑测试
    sh $jd run_0 run_07
    
    还是不懂那就早点休息。。。。
    Signed-off-by: Zhenjian Zhang <itdesk.zhang@gmail.com>
